					<section id="section-831c318d-7c74-41e1-998d-5915763da6b6" data-name="section-general-observer-programs-in-cycle-1" class="section-row none" >
    <div class="component-block container-fluid">
            <div class="row">
                <div class="section-header col-xs-12 text-left">
                    <h2 id="h2-831c318d-7c74-41e1-998d-5915763da6b6" data-name="h2-general-observer-programs-in-cycle-1" class="section-header__title" data-include-in-navigation="true">
                            General Observer Programs in Cycle 1</h2>

                        </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    <div class="component-block container-fluid">
        <p data-index="0" data-name="">&nbsp;</p>

<div class="callout dark-background-stsci-dark-grey callout--size_third pull-right"><span class="sr-only">Callout</span>
<p>The <a href="/files/live/sites/www/files/home/jwst/science-execution/approved-programs/cycle-1-go/_documents/jwst-cycle1-general-observer-abstracts.pdf" >Cycle 1 GO Abstract Catalog </a>&nbsp;is available as a PDF file to facilitate access to this information. <strong>NOTE:</strong>&nbsp; The abstract information is reported as submitted, and may not be up-to-date.</p>
<span class="sr-only">End callout</span></div>

<p>The Cycle 1 General Observers&nbsp;(GO) program provides the worldwide astronomical community with the&nbsp;first extensive opportunity to make observations with JWST. Approximately 6,000 hours were awarded to observing programs using the full suite of JWST instrumentation. Scientists also proposed for archival analysis of data from DD ERS programs and public GTO programs, theoretical investigations, and the&nbsp;development of software tools relevant to JWST observations. Science observations will begin following a 6-month commissioning period after launch.</p>

<p>To view details about a specific program, select a category below, then click the Program ID.&nbsp;For reference:</p>

<ul class="bulleted">
	<li>Small programs: &le; 25 hours</li>
	<li>Medium programs: &gt; 25 and &le; 75 hours</li>
	<li>Large programs: &gt;75 hours</li>
</ul>

<p><strong>NOTE:</strong> The listing of Co-PIs in the tables below has been limited to 4. Proposals with more than 4 Co-PIs are denoted with an asterisk. The full listing is available with the proposal.</p>


<script>hljs.initHighlightingOnLoad();</script>
    </div><div class="component-block container-fluid">
        <div class="accordion" data-module-dynamic="accordion">
            <h3 id="accordion-edb8887d-cedd-41ed-ac74-5c2821dbedff"  class="sr-only">Science Categories for GO Proposals</h3>
            <div class="sr-only" aria-live="polite" aria-atomic="true"></div>
            <div class="accordion__controls">

            </div>
            <ul role="list" aria-labelledby="accordion-edb8887d-cedd-41ed-ac74-5c2821dbedff">
                <li>
                        <div class="accordion-container panel">
    <h4 id="h4-aee976f3-b95a-456a-bf4f-05730e96efb7" data-name="h4-exoplanets-and-exoplanet-formation" class="accordion-header">
        <button class="accordion__section-toggle collapsed accordion-header" id="tab_edb8887d-cedd-41ed-ac74-5c2821dbedff_0_control" data-toggle="collapse" type="button" aria-label="Exoplanets and Exoplanet Formation Navigation Section" aria-controls="tab_edb8887d-cedd-41ed-ac74-5c2821dbedff_0_section" data-target="#tab_edb8887d-cedd-41ed-ac74-5c2821dbedff_0_section"  tabindex="0" aria-expanded="false">

    </h4>

    <div class="accordion__content collapse " aria-expanded="false" id="tab_edb8887d-cedd-41ed-ac74-5c2821dbedff_0_section" aria-labelledby="tab_edb8887d-cedd-41ed-ac74-5c2821dbedff_0_control">

<div class="column-layout__column col-xs-12 col-md-6">
<div class="component-block container-fluid">
<p>BOTS = Bright Object Time-series</p>

<p>FS = Fixed Slit</p>

<p>GTS = Grism Time Series</p>

<p>IFU = Integral Field Unit</p>

<p>LRS = Low Resolution Spectroscopy</p>
</div>
</div>

<div class="column-layout__column col-xs-12 col-md-6">
<div class="component-block container-fluid">
<p>MOS = Multi-object Spectroscopy</p>

<p>MRS = Medium Resolution Spectroscopy</p>

<p>SOSS = Single-object Slitless Spectroscopy</p>

<p>TSO = Time Series Observation</p>

<p>WFSS = Wide Field Slitless Spectroscopy</p>

<script src="https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api.js?render=6Lf1JKUUAAAAADlRmvbTMzYD_fmo83Av-gytnpXw"></script>

<script>
    $(function() {
        // Setup form validation on the #register-form element
        $("#mailing-form-f253740b-8820-4390-9fa9-5892db80652f").validate({
            // Specify the validation rules
            rules: {
                email: {
                    required: true,
                    email: true
                }
            },

            errorElement: "span",
            submitHandler: function() {
                submitForm();
            },
            errorPlacement: function(error, element)
            {
               error.appendTo( $("label[for='" + element.attr('id') + "']") );
               element.attr("aria-describedby", error.attr('id'));
            }
        });
    });

    function submitForm() {
        var $form = $("#mailing-form-f253740b-8820-4390-9fa9-5892db80652f"),
            formAction = $form.attr("action"),
            form = $form[0],
            formData = new FormData(form);

        completeFormSubmission();

        function completeFormSubmission() {
            
            grecaptcha.ready(function() {
                grecaptcha.execute('6Lf1JKUUAAAAADlRmvbTMzYD_fmo83Av-gytnpXw', {action: 'formSubmission'}).then(function(token) {
                    
                    formData.append('g-recaptcha-response', token);
                    formData.append('form-uuid', 'f253740b-8820-4390-9fa9-5892db80652f');

                    
                    var captchaRequest = $.ajax({
                        type: 'POST',
                        url: formAction,
                        data: formData,
                        contentType: false,
                        processData: false,
                        dataType: 'json',
                        traditional: true
                    });

                    captchaRequest.done(function() {
                        var modal = $("#mailing-list-modal-f253740b-8820-4390-9fa9-5892db80652f");
                        modal.find(".timeline-modal-heading").text("Mailing List Confirmation");
                        modal.find(".timeline-modal-description").text("Thank you for subscribing! You will receive a confirmation email shortly.");
                        modal.modal('show');
                        resetForm();
                    });
                    function resetForm() {
                        $form.trigger("reset");
                    }
                });
            });
        }
    }

    $("#email-f253740b-8820-4390-9fa9-5892db80652f").keydown(function(event) {
        if (event.keyCode === 13) {
            event.preventDefault();
            submitForm();
        }
    });
</script></div>
